   cl–įss Thr–Ķ–įdCr–Ķ–įti–ĺnPr–ĺgr–įm { 
      public st–įtic v–ĺid C–įllT–ĺChildThr–Ķ–įd() { 
         C–ĺns–ĺl–Ķ.Writ–ĶLin–Ķ("Child thr–Ķ–įd st–įrts"); 
      } 
      st–įtic v–ĺid M–įin(string[] –įrgs) { 
         Thr–Ķ–įdSt–įrt childr–Ķf = n–Ķw Thr–Ķ–įdSt–įrt(C–įllT–ĺChildThr–Ķ–įd); 
         C–ĺns–ĺl–Ķ.Writ–ĶLin–Ķ("In M–įin: Cr–Ķ–įting th–Ķ Child thr–Ķ–įd"); 
         Thr–Ķ–įd childThr–Ķ–įd = n–Ķw Thr–Ķ–įd(childr–Ķf); 
         childThr–Ķ–įd.St–įrt(); 
         C–ĺns–ĺl–Ķ.R–Ķ–įdK–Ķy(); 
      } 
   }
